[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"VM Periodic Task Thread"[0m[39m [0m[33mos_prio[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[33mcpu[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m39[0m[1;36m.[0m[39m00ms [0m[33melapsed[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m27[0m[1;36m.[0m[39m86s [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [33mtid[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0x000055d261551db0[0m[39m [0m[33mnid[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0x21[0m[39m waiting on condition  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJNI global refs: [0m[1;36m26[0m[39m, weak refs: [0m[1;36m0[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer run on the `CompressTarFuzzer` harness triggered a timeout after [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapproximately [0m[1;36m28[0m[39m seconds. The thread dump shows the main thread spending its entire[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCPU time inside Java’s big-integer and big-decimal division routines, invoked from [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe Apache Commons Compress TAR‐handling classes, specifically during Pax header [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing in `TarArchiveEntry.parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds`.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• What the issue is  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – During fuzz testing, certain inputs cause the TAR archive parser to enter an [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextremely long or infinite computation, ultimately leading libFuzzer to report a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“timeout.”  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – No exception or crash occurs; rather, the process remains busy [0m[1;39m([0m[39m“RUNNABLE”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minside arithmetic routines.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – Although no security defect such as a crash or exception is directly reported, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe behavior constitutes a performance hang or potential denial-of-service—fuzzed [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minputs can stall the parser indefinitely.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Important observations and findings  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The main thread is engaged in `java.math.MutableBigInteger.divideOneWord` → [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`divideKnuth` → `BigInteger.divideAndRemainderKnuth` → `BigDecimal.divideAndRound` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m→ `BigDecimal.divide` → `BigDecimal.divideToIntegralValue` → [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`BigDecimal.remainder`.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. This arithmetic chain is rooted in [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarArchiveEntry.parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m277[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which is called while [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing Pax headers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`processPaxHeader`, `updateEntryFromPaxHeaders`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The TAR file driver [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TarFile.<init>`, `applyPaxHeadersToCurrentEntry`, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`getNextTarEntry`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m feeds into the fuzzer entry point at [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. No other threads are blocked; this is pure CPU consumption in numeric division[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than a synchronization deadlock.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Code areas to investigate  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString decimalSeconds[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `TarArchiveEntry.processPaxHeader` and `updateEntryFromPaxHeaders`  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `TarFile` constructors and methods around Pax header application [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`applyPaxHeadersToCurrentEntry`, `paxHeaders`, `getNextTarEntry`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Big-number routines invoked:  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • `BigDecimal.createAndStripZerosToMatchScale`  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • `BigDecimal.divideAndRound` [0m[35m/[0m[39m `divide` [0m[35m/[0m[39m `divideToIntegralValue` [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`remainder`  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • Underlying `MutableBigInteger.divideKnuth` implementations  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInvestigating these parts will give a holistic view of why certain [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecimal‐to‐instant conversions can consume unbounded time under malformed or [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madversarial inputs.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfractional parts drive Knuth’s division routines into pathological worst‐case time.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing logic for parsing the integer part [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mlongValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and computing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnanoseconds via scaling must remain intact for valid inputs. We only wish to reject[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor truncate pathological fractional lengths, not alter correct behavior for typical[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPAX timestamps.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Constrain fractional precision at validation time  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Modify the regex `PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN` so that it only [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatches up to [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m digits after the decimal point [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnanosecond precision[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Original [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m221[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m223[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d*[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Revised:  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m0,9[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. This change rejects any header value with more than [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m fractional digits, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreventing pathological `BigDecimal.scale` values from ever reaching the arithmetic[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Add a defensive scale‐check immediately after BigDecimal construction  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Even with the tightened regex, on the off‐chance of bypass or future regex [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdrift, explicitly guard against excessive scale. Insert after `new [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mBigDecimal[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjust before `long seconds = [0m[33m...[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mepochSeconds.scale[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Corrupted PAX header. Time field has too many [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mdecimal places: '"[0m[39m + value + [0m[32m"'"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This direct check is constant‐time [0m[1;39m([0m[39mscale is a metadata field[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and immediately[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maborts mis­formatted inputs, preserving the precise scale requirement.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. No other code changes  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not touch BigDecimal arithmetic calls, TAR‐harness, fuzzing entry points, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor utility functions.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing tests expecting up to [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m‐digit fractions will still pass; inputs with [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlonger fractions are now correctly refused.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification and side‐effect mitigation  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By bounding fractional digits to [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m, we guarantee that remainder and shift [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations operate in at most [0m[1;35mO[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m digit‐length [0m[1;39m([0m[39msingle‐word[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m arithmetic, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminating unbounded CPU consumption.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The integer‐part extraction [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mlongValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and fractional‐to‐nanos [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalculation remain unchanged and correct for all valid PAX timestamps.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any malicious or malformed header with excessive precision is now rejected [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mearly, consistent with the PAX specification’s intention of nanosecond resolution. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach avoids complex custom parsing or any slow‐path arithmetic; it is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man in‐place fix, minimal in scope, and does not touch harness or external [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdependencies.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References to changes  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Relevant code file: [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.java`  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Code ranges updated:  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Pattern definition around lines [0m[1;36m221[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m223[0m[39m  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Validation logic around lines [0m[1;36m275[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m277[0m[39m  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
